{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KHW4dC4PyrnKCRbWvMkw8e","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01TeKGNsjjLHVGui3EQ8SphY","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md","content":"# Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Overview\n\nThis release introduces significant API improvements focused on improving the evaluation service architecture, expanding authentication options, and enhancing segment handling with multi-segment support. The changes reflect Flipt's evolution toward a more flexible and scalable feature flag management system.\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading. Refer to the Upgrade Guide for detailed migration instructions.\n\n### Evaluation API Architecture Redesign\n\n**Affected Components:** gRPC Evaluation Service, REST API\n\nThe legacy `Evaluate` and `BatchEvaluate` RPC methods in the core `Flipt` service are now **deprecated** in favor of the new dedicated `EvaluationService`.\n\n- **Old API** (deprecated): `rpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)` and `rpc BatchEvaluate(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)` in the `flipt.Flipt` service\n- **New API** (recommended): Use the `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService` with separate methods:\n  - `rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)`\n  - `rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)`\n  - `rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)`\n\n**REST Endpoints:**\n- `POST /evaluate/v1/boolean` — Evaluate a boolean flag\n- `POST /evaluate/v1/variant` — Evaluate a variant flag\n- `POST /evaluate/v1/batch` — Batch evaluate multiple requests\n\n**Impact:** The new API provides stronger type safety (separate response types for boolean vs. variant evaluations) and a cleaner separation of concerns. Clients must migrate to the new endpoints.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Update gRPC clients to use `EvaluationService` instead of `Flipt` service for evaluations\n2. Update REST clients to use `/evaluate/v1/boolean`, `/evaluate/v1/variant`, and `/evaluate/v1/batch` instead of the legacy evaluation endpoints\n3. Update your request payloads to use the new `EvaluationRequest` from `flipt.evaluation` package (includes `namespace_key` as first-class field and `reference` for git references)\n4. Update response handling to expect typed responses: `BooleanEvaluationResponse` or `VariantEvaluationResponse` with specific fields for each flag type\n\n### Multi-Segment Support via Deprecated `segment_key` Field\n\n**Affected Components:** Rules API, Rollouts API, Evaluation Response\n\nThe `segment_key` field is **deprecated** across multiple request and response types in favor of `segment_keys` (plural) with an explicit `segment_operator` (AND/OR).\n\n**Deprecated Fields:**\n- `Rule.segment_key` → Use `Rule.segment_keys` (array) + `Rule.segment_operator`\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_key` → Use `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` (array) + `RolloutSegment.segment_operator`\n- `CreateRuleRequest.segment_key` → Use `CreateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `CreateRuleRequest.segment_operator`\n- `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_key` → Use `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_operator`\n- `EvaluationResponse.segment_key` → Use `EvaluationResponse.segment_keys` (array)\n\n**Impact:** Rules and rollouts can now reference multiple segments with explicit AND/OR logic instead of being restricted to a single segment.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. For single-segment rules: Convert `segment_key: \"my_segment\"` to `segment_keys: [\"my_segment\"]` and set `segment_operator: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR`\n2. For multiple segments: Use the new `segment_keys` array with the appropriate operator:\n   - `AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` — Entity must match all segments\n   - `OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` — Entity must match at least one segment\n3. Update response parsing to use `segment_keys` instead of `segment_key`\n\n**Example Migration:**\n```protobuf\n// Before\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;  // deprecated\n  int32 rank = 3;\n}\n\n// After\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6;\n}\n```\n\n### Pagination API Deprecation (Offset → Page Token)\n\n**Affected Components:** List APIs\n\nThe `offset` field in list requests is deprecated in favor of cursor-based pagination using `page_token`:\n- `ListFlagRequest.offset` → Use `ListFlagRequest.page_token`\n- `ListNamespaceRequest.offset` → Use `ListNamespaceRequest.page_token`\n- `ListSegmentRequest.offset` → Use `ListSegmentRequest.page_token`\n- `ListRuleRequest.offset` → Use `ListRuleRequest.page_token`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Replace offset-based pagination with cursor-based pagination\n2. Retrieve the `next_page_token` from list responses and use it for subsequent requests\n3. Continue until `next_page_token` is empty\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### New Evaluation Service with Typed Responses\n\n**Component:** `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`\n\nThe dedicated evaluation service provides type-safe evaluation through separate endpoints for boolean and variant flags:\n\n**Boolean Evaluation:**\n```bash\nPOST /evaluate/v1/boolean\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_boolean_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-123\",\n  \"context\": {\n    \"plan\": \"enterprise\",\n    \"region\": \"us-east-1\"\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  \"enabled\": true,\n  \"reason\": \"MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\",\n  \"request_id\": \"...\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_boolean_flag\",\n  \"request_duration_millis\": 1.5,\n  \"timestamp\": \"2024-04-11T15:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Variant Evaluation:**\n```bash\nPOST /evaluate/v1/variant\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_variant_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-123\",\n  \"context\": {\n    \"plan\": \"enterprise\"\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  \"match\": true,\n  \"variant_key\": \"control\",\n  \"variant_attachment\": \"{\\\"url\\\": \\\"...\\\"}\"\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"premium_users\"],\n  \"reason\": \"MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\",\n  \"request_id\": \"...\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_variant_flag\",\n  \"request_duration_millis\": 1.2,\n  \"timestamp\": \"2024-04-11T15:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Batch Evaluation:**\n```bash\nPOST /evaluate/v1/batch\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"request_id\": \"batch-123\",\n  \"requests\": [\n    {\"namespace_key\": \"default\", \"flag_key\": \"feature_a\", \"entity_id\": \"user-123\", ...},\n    {\"namespace_key\": \"default\", \"flag_key\": \"feature_b\", \"entity_id\": \"user-123\", ...}\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Multi-Segment Rules and Rollouts\n\n**Components:** `Rule`, `RolloutSegment`, `CreateRuleRequest`, `UpdateRuleRequest`, `CreateRolloutRequest`, `UpdateRolloutRequest`\n\nRules and rollouts now support multiple segments with explicit boolean logic:\n\n```protobuf\nmessage Rule {\n  string id = 1;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 9;      // NEW: Array of segment keys\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 10; // NEW: AND/OR logic\n  ...\n}\n\nenum SegmentOperator {\n  OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR = 0;  // Match any segment (default, backward compatible)\n  AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR = 1; // Match all segments\n}\n```\n\n**API Example:**\n```bash\nPOST /api/v1/flags/my_flag/rules\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"premium_users\", \"beta_testers\"],\n  \"segment_operator\": \"AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\",\n  \"rank\": 1\n}\n```\n\nThis rule now requires an entity to match BOTH \"premium_users\" AND \"beta_testers\" segments.\n\n### GitHub OAuth Authentication Method\n\n**Component:** `flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodGithubService`\n\nAdded GitHub OAuth 2.0 support as an alternative to OIDC:\n\n**Endpoints:**\n- `GET /auth/v1/method/github/authorize?provider=<provider>&state=<state>` — Initiate OAuth flow\n- `GET /auth/v1/method/github/callback?provider=<provider>&code=<code>&state=<state>` — Complete OAuth flow\n\n**Features:**\n- Support for GitHub organization membership verification\n- Configurable team membership checks for fine-grained access control\n- Session-compatible authentication (compatible with HTTP cookies)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    github:\n      enabled: true\n      clients:\n        my-github-app:\n          client_id: \"your-github-app-id\"\n          client_secret: \"your-github-app-secret\"\n          org: \"my-organization\"     # Optional: require membership\n          teams: [\"developers\"]      # Optional: require team membership\n```\n\n### Data Service for Evaluation Snapshots\n\n**Component:** `flipt.evaluation.DataService`\n\nNew service provides read-only evaluation data snapshots:\n\n**Endpoint:**\n- `rpc EvaluationSnapshotNamespace(EvaluationNamespaceSnapshotRequest) returns (EvaluationNamespaceSnapshot)`\n\nReturns a complete snapshot of all flags, rules, rollouts, and constraints for a namespace, useful for:\n- Caching evaluation data\n- Building client-side SDKs\n- Auditing flag configurations\n\n**Response Structure:**\n```protobuf\nmessage EvaluationNamespaceSnapshot {\n  EvaluationNamespace namespace = 1;\n  repeated EvaluationFlag flags = 2;  // All flags with rules, rollouts, and constraints\n}\n```\n\n### OCI Storage Improvements\n\n**Component:** Internal Storage (OCI/Container Registry support)\n\n- **Better AWS ECR Integration**: Improved compatibility and performance when using Flipt with AWS Elastic Container Registry\n- **Configurable OCI Manifest Versions**: Support for different OCI manifest versions for better registry compatibility\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: \"my-registry.azurecr.io/flipt-config\"\n    manifest_version: \"1.1\"  # or \"1.0\"\n```\n\n### File System (Git) Storage Enhancements\n\n**Component:** Git-based File System Storage\n\n- **Directory Scope Support**: Flipt can now scope git repository configuration to specific directories within the repository\n- Enables using a single git repository for multiple Flipt deployments with isolated configurations\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: git\n  git:\n    repository: \"https://github.com/my-org/configs.git\"\n    ref: \"main\"\n    directory: \"flipt/production\"  # NEW: Scope to subdirectory\n```\n\n### Validation Command Improvements\n\n**Component:** CLI\n\n- **Working Directory Parameter**: The `flipt validate` command now accepts a working directory parameter for more flexible validation workflows\n\n**Usage:**\n```bash\nflipt validate --config /etc/flipt/config.yml --dir /path/to/working/dir\n```\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Legacy Evaluation API\n\n**Deprecated:** `flipt.Flipt.Evaluate()` and `flipt.Flipt.BatchEvaluate()`\n\n**Replacement:** Use `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService.Boolean()`, `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService.Variant()`, and `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService.Batch()`\n\n**Timeline:** The legacy API will be removed in a future major release (approximately 1 year from v1.40.0)\n\n### Single Segment Fields\n\n**Deprecated:**\n- `Rule.segment_key`\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_key`\n- `CreateRuleRequest.segment_key`\n- `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_key`\n- `EvaluationResponse.segment_key`\n\n**Replacement:** Use the plural `segment_keys` field with explicit `segment_operator`\n\n**Timeline:** Will be removed in a future major release (approximately 1 year from v1.40.0)\n\n### Offset-Based Pagination\n\n**Deprecated:** `offset` field in list requests\n- `ListFlagRequest.offset`\n- `ListNamespaceRequest.offset`\n- `ListSegmentRequest.offset`\n- `ListRuleRequest.offset`\n\n**Replacement:** Use cursor-based `page_token` pagination\n\n**Timeline:** Will be removed in a future major release (approximately 1 year from v1.13.0)\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter\n\n**Deprecated Since:** v1.36.0\n\n**Status:** No longer supported; OpenTelemetry dropped support for the Jaeger exporter in July 2023.\n\n**Replacement:** Configure direct OTLP export to Jaeger or use OpenTelemetry Collector\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### Evaluation System\n\n- Fixed `isnotoneof` operator using incorrect comparison logic\n- Fixed issue with segment constraints when constraints belong to the same segment key in different namespaces\n- Fixed JSON schema validation for `key`/`keys` fields in rollout segment definitions\n- Improved error handling in evaluator to prevent panics during malformed flag evaluation\n\n### Authentication & Caching\n\n- **Authentication**: Skip establishing database connection when authentication is not configured, reducing unnecessary resource usage\n- **Cache**: Fixed cache eviction to only store authentication hash instead of full credentials\n- **Cache**: Added support for username parameter in Redis configuration for secure authentication\n\n### UI/UX\n\n- **Evaluation Console**: Now provides warnings when context values may cause unexpected evaluation results\n- Improved user guidance for context-dependent flag evaluation\n\n### Configuration & Logging\n\n- Fixed invalid trace log level schema that could prevent proper tracing configuration\n- Improved configuration validation to catch malformed settings earlier\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\nFollow these steps to upgrade to this release:\n\n### Step 1: Review Breaking Changes\n\nRead the \"Breaking Changes\" section above and identify which parts of your deployment are affected:\n- [ ] Do you use the gRPC `Flipt.Evaluate()` or `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` methods?\n- [ ] Do you use REST API evaluation endpoints other than `/evaluate/v1/*`?\n- [ ] Do you use `segment_key` (singular) in rule or rollout creation?\n- [ ] Do you use offset-based pagination in list APIs?\n\n### Step 2: Update Client SDKs and Applications\n\n**For gRPC Clients:**\n1. Update your protobuf definitions from the latest v1.40.0+ release\n2. Replace calls to `Flipt.Evaluate()` with `EvaluationService.Boolean()` or `EvaluationService.Variant()`\n3. Replace calls to `Flipt.BatchEvaluate()` with `EvaluationService.Batch()`\n4. Update your request objects to use the new `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationRequest` struct\n5. Update response handling for strongly-typed `BooleanEvaluationResponse` and `VariantEvaluationResponse`\n\n**For REST Clients:**\n1. Replace requests to `/api/evaluate` (legacy) with:\n   - `/evaluate/v1/boolean` for boolean flags\n   - `/evaluate/v1/variant` for variant flags\n   - `/evaluate/v1/batch` for batch evaluations\n2. Ensure your request body includes `namespace_key` at the top level (was previously optional)\n3. Update response parsing for the new typed response structures\n\n**For Pagination:**\n1. Replace offset-based pagination:\n   ```javascript\n   // Before\n   GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\n\n   // After\n   GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=<token_from_previous_response>\n   ```\n\n### Step 3: Update Flipt Configuration (if applicable)\n\nIf you're using any deprecated configuration options:\n\n1. **Git Storage with Directory Scope** (optional enhancement):\n   ```yaml\n   # Old (still works)\n   storage:\n     type: git\n     git:\n       repository: \"https://github.com/my-org/configs.git\"\n\n   # New (optional)\n   storage:\n     type: git\n     git:\n       repository: \"https://github.com/my-org/configs.git\"\n       directory: \"flipt/prod\"  # NEW: Add directory scope\n   ```\n\n2. **OCI Storage with Manifest Version** (optional):\n   ```yaml\n   storage:\n     type: oci\n     oci:\n       repository: \"my-registry.azurecr.io/flipt-config\"\n       manifest_version: \"1.1\"  # NEW: Specify manifest version\n   ```\n\n### Step 4: Update Rules and Rollouts (Multi-Segment Support)\n\nIf you have existing rules or rollouts with single segments, they will continue to work with the default `OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR`. To take advantage of multi-segment support:\n\n1. **Via API:**\n   ```bash\n   # Old: Single segment\n   POST /api/v1/flags/my_flag/rules\n   {\n     \"segment_key\": \"premium_users\",\n     \"rank\": 1\n   }\n\n   # New: Multiple segments with AND logic\n   POST /api/v1/flags/my_flag/rules\n   {\n     \"segment_keys\": [\"premium_users\", \"beta_testers\"],\n     \"segment_operator\": \"AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\",\n     \"rank\": 1\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Via UI**: The Flipt UI will guide you when creating or editing rules\n\n### Step 5: Add GitHub Authentication (Optional)\n\nIf you want to enable GitHub OAuth:\n\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    github:\n      enabled: true\n      clients:\n        github-oauth:\n          client_id: \"${GITHUB_CLIENT_ID}\"\n          client_secret: \"${GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET}\"\n          scopes:\n            - \"read:org\"\n          org: \"my-organization\"      # Optional: require org membership\n          teams: [\"developers\"]       # Optional: require team membership\n```\n\n### Step 6: Test the Upgrade\n\n1. **In Development/Staging:**\n   - Deploy the new version alongside the old version for validation\n   - Run integration tests against new evaluation endpoints\n   - Verify authentication methods still work\n   - Test pagination with `page_token`\n\n2. **Smoke Tests:**\n   ```bash\n   # Test new evaluation API\n   curl -X POST http://localhost:8080/evaluate/v1/boolean \\\n     -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n     -d '{\"namespace_key\":\"default\",\"flag_key\":\"test_flag\",\"entity_id\":\"user-1\"}'\n\n   # Test list API pagination\n   curl \"http://localhost:8080/api/v1/flags?limit=10\" \\\n     -H \"Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN\"\n   ```\n\n3. **Gradual Rollout:**\n   - Update client applications one service at a time\n   - Monitor logs for any deprecated API usage warnings\n   - Verify evaluation latency and accuracy\n\n### Step 7: Plan Decommission of Legacy APIs (Optional)\n\nPlan for removal of deprecated APIs in your roadmap:\n- Set a date for discontinuing support of legacy evaluation endpoints (suggested: 12+ months out)\n- Audit your applications for remaining usage of deprecated fields\n- Create a tracking issue for complete migration\n\n### Rollback Plan\n\nIf issues arise:\n1. Revert to the previous stable version\n2. Check error logs and metrics to identify the issue\n3. Report any issues at https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues\n4. Re-test before attempting the upgrade again\n\n### Support\n\n- **Documentation**: https://www.flipt.io/docs\n- **GitHub Issues**: https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues\n- **Discussions**: https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/discussions\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThis release modernizes Flipt's evaluation API with better type safety, introduces powerful multi-segment support for complex targeting rules, expands authentication options with GitHub OAuth, and improves storage flexibility. While there are breaking changes, the migration path is straightforward, and the improvements provide a stronger foundation for feature flag management at scale.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1040,"cache_read_input_tokens":74753,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1040},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"24914559-d354-40e7-b50b-fdf1adc79508","uuid":"e06aa006-4a51-4597-a0bf-ed169ca0b31b"}

The changes reflect Flipt's evolution toward a more flexible and scalable feature flag management system.\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\n> These changes require action from users upgrading. Refer to the Upgrade Guide for detailed migration instructions.\n\n### Evaluation API Architecture Redesign\n\n**Affected Components:** gRPC Evaluation Service, REST API\n\nThe legacy `Evaluate` and `BatchEvaluate` RPC methods in the core `Flipt` service are now **deprecated** in favor of the new dedicated `EvaluationService`.\n\n- **Old API** (deprecated): `rpc Evaluate(EvaluationRequest) returns (EvaluationResponse)` and `rpc BatchEvaluate(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)` in the `flipt.Flipt` service\n- **New API** (recommended): Use the `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService` with separate methods:\n  - `rpc Boolean(EvaluationRequest) returns (BooleanEvaluationResponse)`\n  - `rpc Variant(EvaluationRequest) returns (VariantEvaluationResponse)`\n  - `rpc Batch(BatchEvaluationRequest) returns (BatchEvaluationResponse)`\n\n**REST Endpoints:**\n- `POST /evaluate/v1/boolean` — Evaluate a boolean flag\n- `POST /evaluate/v1/variant` — Evaluate a variant flag\n- `POST /evaluate/v1/batch` — Batch evaluate multiple requests\n\n**Impact:** The new API provides stronger type safety (separate response types for boolean vs. variant evaluations) and a cleaner separation of concerns. Clients must migrate to the new endpoints.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Update gRPC clients to use `EvaluationService` instead of `Flipt` service for evaluations\n2. Update REST clients to use `/evaluate/v1/boolean`, `/evaluate/v1/variant`, and `/evaluate/v1/batch` instead of the legacy evaluation endpoints\n3. Update your request payloads to use the new `EvaluationRequest` from `flipt.evaluation` package (includes `namespace_key` as first-class field and `reference` for git references)\n4. Update response handling to expect typed responses: `BooleanEvaluationResponse` or `VariantEvaluationResponse` with specific fields for each flag type\n\n### Multi-Segment Support via Deprecated `segment_key` Field\n\n**Affected Components:** Rules API, Rollouts API, Evaluation Response\n\nThe `segment_key` field is **deprecated** across multiple request and response types in favor of `segment_keys` (plural) with an explicit `segment_operator` (AND/OR).\n\n**Deprecated Fields:**\n- `Rule.segment_key` → Use `Rule.segment_keys` (array) + `Rule.segment_operator`\n- `RolloutSegment.segment_key` → Use `RolloutSegment.segment_keys` (array) + `RolloutSegment.segment_operator`\n- `CreateRuleRequest.segment_key` → Use `CreateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `CreateRuleRequest.segment_operator`\n- `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_key` → Use `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_keys` + `UpdateRuleRequest.segment_operator`\n- `EvaluationResponse.segment_key` → Use `EvaluationResponse.segment_keys` (array)\n\n**Impact:** Rules and rollouts can now reference multiple segments with explicit AND/OR logic instead of being restricted to a single segment.\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. For single-segment rules: Convert `segment_key: \"my_segment\"` to `segment_keys: [\"my_segment\"]` and set `segment_operator: OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR`\n2. For multiple segments: Use the new `segment_keys` array with the appropriate operator:\n   - `AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` — Entity must match all segments\n   - `OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` — Entity must match at least one segment\n3. Update response parsing to use `segment_keys` instead of `segment_key`\n\n**Example Migration:**\n```protobuf\n// Before\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  string segment_key = 2;  // deprecated\n  int32 rank = 3;\n}\n\n// After\nmessage CreateRuleRequest {\n  string flag_key = 1;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 5;\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 6;\n}\n```\n\n### Pagination API Deprecation (Offset → Page Token)\n\n**Affected Components:** List APIs\n\nThe `offset` field in list requests is deprecated in favor of cursor-based pagination using `page_token`:\n- `ListFlagRequest.offset` → Use `ListFlagRequest.page_token`\n- `ListNamespaceRequest.offset` → Use `ListNamespaceRequest.page_token`\n- `ListSegmentRequest.offset` → Use `ListSegmentRequest.page_token`\n- `ListRuleRequest.offset` → Use `ListRuleRequest.page_token`\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Replace offset-based pagination with cursor-based pagination\n2. Retrieve the `next_page_token` from list responses and use it for subsequent requests\n3. Continue until `next_page_token` is empty\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### New Evaluation Service with Typed Responses\n\n**Component:** `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService`\n\nThe dedicated evaluation service provides type-safe evaluation through separate endpoints for boolean and variant flags:\n\n**Boolean Evaluation:**\n```bash\nPOST /evaluate/v1/boolean\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_boolean_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-123\",\n  \"context\": {\n    \"plan\": \"enterprise\",\n    \"region\": \"us-east-1\"\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  \"enabled\": true,\n  \"reason\": \"MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\",\n  \"request_id\": \"...\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_boolean_flag\",\n  \"request_duration_millis\": 1.5,\n  \"timestamp\": \"2024-04-11T15:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Variant Evaluation:**\n```bash\nPOST /evaluate/v1/variant\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_variant_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-123\",\n  \"context\": {\n    \"plan\": \"enterprise\"\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  \"match\": true,\n  \"variant_key\": \"control\",\n  \"variant_attachment\": \"{\\\"url\\\": \\\"...\\\"}\"\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"premium_users\"],\n  \"reason\": \"MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\",\n  \"request_id\": \"...\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_variant_flag\",\n  \"request_duration_millis\": 1.2,\n  \"timestamp\": \"2024-04-11T15:30:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Batch Evaluation:**\n```bash\nPOST /evaluate/v1/batch\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"request_id\": \"batch-123\",\n  \"requests\": [\n    {\"namespace_key\": \"default\", \"flag_key\": \"feature_a\", \"entity_id\": \"user-123\", ...},\n    {\"namespace_key\": \"default\", \"flag_key\": \"feature_b\", \"entity_id\": \"user-123\", ...}\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n### Multi-Segment Rules and Rollouts\n\n**Components:** `Rule`, `RolloutSegment`, `CreateRuleRequest`, `UpdateRuleRequest`, `CreateRolloutRequest`, `UpdateRolloutRequest`\n\nRules and rollouts now support multiple segments with explicit boolean logic:\n\n```protobuf\nmessage Rule {\n  string id = 1;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 9;      // NEW: Array of segment keys\n  SegmentOperator segment_operator = 10; // NEW: AND/OR logic\n  ...\n}\n\nenum SegmentOperator {\n  OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR = 0;  // Match any segment (default, backward compatible)\n  AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR = 1; // Match all segments\n}\n```\n\n**API Example:**\n```bash\nPOST /api/v1/flags/my_flag/rules\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"premium_users\", \"beta_testers\"],\n  \"segment_operator\": \"AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\",\n  \"rank\": 1\n}\n```\n\nThis rule now requires an entity to match BOTH \"premium_users\" AND \"beta_testers\" segments.\n\n### GitHub OAuth Authentication Method\n\n**Component:** `flipt.auth.AuthenticationMethodGithubService`\n\nAdded GitHub OAuth 2.0 support as an alternative to OIDC:\n\n**Endpoints:**\n- `GET /auth/v1/method/github/authorize?provider=<provider>&state=<state>` — Initiate OAuth flow\n- `GET /auth/v1/method/github/callback?provider=<provider>&code=<code>&state=<state>` — Complete OAuth flow\n\n**Features:**\n- Support for GitHub organization membership verification\n- Configurable team membership checks for fine-grained access control\n- Session-compatible authentication (compatible with HTTP cookies)\n\n**Configuration Example:**\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    github:\n      enabled: true\n      clients:\n        my-github-app:\n          client_id: \"your-github-app-id\"\n          client_secret: \"your-github-app-secret\"\n          org: \"my-organization\"     # Optional: require membership\n          teams: [\"developers\"]      # Optional: require team membership\n```\n\n### Data Service for Evaluation Snapshots\n\n**Component:** `flipt.evaluation.DataService`\n\nNew service provides read-only evaluation data and constraints for a namespace, useful for:\n- Caching evaluation data\n- Building client-side SDKs\n- Auditing flag configurations\n\n**Response Structure:**\n```protobuf\nmessage Replace offset-based pagination:\n   ```javascript\n   // Before\n   GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&offset=20\n\n   // After\n   GET /api/v1/flags?limit=10&page_token=<token_from_previous_response>\n   ```\n\n### Step 3: Update Flipt Configuration (if applicable)\n\nIf you're using any deprecated configuration options:\n\n1. **Git Storage with Directory Scope** (optional enhancement):\n   ```yaml\n   # Old (still works)\n   storage:\n     type: git\n     git:\n       repository: \"https://github.com/my-org/configs.git\"\n\n   # New (optional)\n   storage:\n     type: git\n     git:\n       repository: \"https://github.com/my-org/configs.git\"\n       directory: \"flipt/prod\"  # NEW: Add directory scope\n   ```\n\n2. **OCI Storage with Manifest Version** (optional):\n   ```yaml\n   storage:\n     type: oci\n     oci:\n       repository: \"my-registry.azurecr.io/flipt-config\"\n       manifest_version: \"1.1\"  # NEW: Specify manifest version\n   ```\n\n### Step 4: Update Rules and Rollouts (Multi-Segment Support)\n\nIf you have existing rules or rollouts with single segments, they will continue to work with the default `OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR`. To take advantage of multi-segment support:\n\n1. **Via API:**\n   ```bash\n   # Old: Single segment\n   POST /api/v1/flags/my_flag/rules\n   {\n     \"segment_key\": \"premium_users\",\n     \"rank\": 1\n   }\n\n   # New: Multiple segments with AND logic\n   POST /api/v1/flags/my_flag/rules\n   {\n     \"segment_keys\": [\"premium_users\", \"beta_testers\"],\n     \"segment_operator\": \"AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR\",\n     \"rank\": 1\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Via UI**: The Flipt UI will guide you when creating or editing rules\n\n### Step 5: Add GitHub Authentication (Optional)\n\nIf you want to enable GitHub OAuth:\n\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    github:\n      enabled: true\n      clients:\n        github-oauth:\n          client_id: \"${GITHUB_CLIENT_ID}\"\n          client_secret: \"${GITHUB_CLIENT_SECRET}\"\n          scopes:\n            -
